1693<h2>

1694<strong>

1695Browse Our</strong>

1696 <strong>

16972021</strong>

1698&nbsp;<strong>

1699Collection of Cabinet Hardware</strong>

1700&nbsp;</h2>

1701

1702

1703<p>

1704Our collection features styles available in multiple finishes such as brass, polished nickel, oil-rubbed bronze, and more. Whether you&rsquo;re looking for a rustic look, transitional, or contemporary, we have the perfect pulls and knobs for your cabinetry. Browse the collection now or read tips on <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-to-choose-cabinet-hardware/" target="_blank">

1705how to choose cabinet hardware</a>

1706.&nbsp;</p>

1707

1708

1709<h3>

1710Cabinet Hardware</h3>

1711

1712

1713<p>

1714<em>

1715<strong>

1716Cabinet hardware</strong>

1717</em>

1718 is classified into two main types: pulls and knobs. Use one type or both, each have certain qualities and styles that make them useful and beautiful.&nbsp;</p>

1719

1720

1721<ul>

1722

1723 <li>

1724<em>

1725<strong>

1726Cabinet pulls</strong>

1727</em>

1728 also referred to as handles, typically longer than a knob. These are available in multiple designs including bar, cup, arch, handle, and others.<br />

1729

1730 &nbsp;</li>

1731

1732 <li>

1733<em>

1734<strong>

1735Cabinet knobs</strong>

1736</em>

1737 are typically smaller than a pull, coming in styles like birdcage, round, oval, square, rectangle, and other shapes to match your cabinets.&nbsp;</li>

1738

1739</ul>

1740

1741

1742<p>

1743Both styles are available multiple finishes such as chrome, brushed nickel, brass, black, stainless steel, and more. To find matching sets, we recommend shopping by collection or by finish as your browse. If you have questions or would like an opinion on hardware for your cabinets, <a href="mailto:design@vevano.com" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">

1744<u>

1745contact</u>

1746</a>

1747 our design experts. &nbsp;</p>

1748
